```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

```swift
struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }
    }
}

struct Reader: View {
    let blocks: [MarkdownBlock]
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView {
            ForEach(blocks.indices, id: \.self) { i in
                BlockView(block: blocks[i])
            }
        }

}
